brjod pa yang rig par bgyid do / /
tshe dang ldan pa khyod dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye byed par spro'am /
spro'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye bgyid par spro na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang ba mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye bgyid par bsko ste /
dge slong dgag dbye bgyid pa ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye bgyid par 'gyur ro / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye bgyid par spro ste /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye bgyid par bsko na /
dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye bgyid par bsko bar /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsungs shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi bar dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye bgyid par bskos lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
deng dge 'dun gyi dgag dbye bco lnga pa lags te /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang ba mdzod cig dang /
deng dge 'dun dgag dbye mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
deng dge 'dun gyi dgag dbye bco lnga pa lags la /
bdag cag dge 'dun thams cad ni ltung ba dang bcas par gyur na /
gang gi mdun du bdag cag ltung ba de chos bzhin du slar bgyi ba bdag cag la dge slong gnas gzhan du mchis la /
dge slong gi mdun du ltung ba de chos bzhin du slar bgyid par spro ba su yang ma mchis na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis deng ltung ba de byin gyis brlabs te dgag dbye mdzad la /
slad kyi dge slong gi mdun du ltung ba de chos bzhin du slar mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
deng dge 'dun gyi dgag dbye bco lnga pa lags la /
bdag cag dge 'dun thams cad ni ltung ba la dogs pa dang yid gnyis dang bcas par gyur na /
gang gi mdun du bdag cag ltung ba de chos bzhin du slar bgyi ba bdag cag las dge slong gnas gzhan du mchis la /
dge slong mdo sde 'dzin pa dang 'dul ba 'dzin pa dang ma mo 'dzin pa rnams la dris te dogs pa dang yid gnyis bsal la ltung ba de chos bzhin du slar bgyid par spro ba su yang ma mchis na gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na /
dge 'dun gyis gnang ba mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dang ltung ba de byin gyis brlabs te dgag dbye mdzad la /
slad kyi dge slong mdo sde 'dzin pa dang 'dul ba 'dzin pa dang ma mo 'dzin pa rnams la dris te dogs pa dang yid gnyis bsal la /
ltung ba de chos bzhin du slar mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
deng dge 'dun gyi dgag dbye bco lnga pa lags la /
bdag cag dge 'dun thams cad ni ltung ba'i slad du rtsod par gyur pa na /
gal te dge 'dun gyis dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis deng ltung ba'i slad du rtsod pa byin gyis brlabs te dgag dbye mdzad la slad kyi dge slong mdo sde 'dzin pa dang 'dul ba 'dzin pa dang ma mo 'dzin pa rnams la dris te rtsod pa zhi bar bgyis la ltung ba de chos bzhin du slar mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
deng dge 'dun gyi dgag dbye bco lnga pa la /
bdag cag dge 'dun thams cad ni ltung ba la nges pa nyid ma lags par gyur na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis deng ltung ba la nges pa nyid ma lags pa de byin gyis brlabs te dgag dbye mdzad la /
slad kyi dge slong mdo sde 'dzin pa dang 'dul ba 'dzin pa dang ma mo 'dzin pa rnams la dris te nges pa nyid ma lags pa bsal la ltung ba de chos bzhin du slar mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
tshe dang ldan pa dgongs su gsol /
deng dge 'dun gyi dgag dbye bco lnga pa lags te /
bdag dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba'i dgag dbye yang bco lnga pa lags na /
bdag dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba bdag la mthong ba dang thos pa dang dogs pa'i gnas gsum gyis dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye bgyid kyis /
tshe dang ldan pa rnams kyis bdag la gdams su gsol /
tshe dang ldan pa rnams kyis bdag la rjes su bstan du gsol /
tshe dang ldan pa rnams kyis bdag la rjes su gzung du gsol /
thugs brtse ba can tshe dang ldan pa rnams kyis thugs brtse ba'i slad du bdag la thugs brtse bar mdzad du gsol /
ltung ba shes shing mthong na chos bzhin 'dul ba bzhin du slar bgyi'o / /
lan gsum du bzlas /
thabs yin no / /
legs so / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
'di ltar gnas 'di na dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyis dgag dbye mdzad lags so / /
legs par dgag dbye mdzad do / /
shin tu dgag dbye mdzad do / /
btsun pa rdzas 'di lta bus kyang dbyar gnas pa'i dge slong gi dge 'dun la dgag dbye bgyir rung ngo / /
de'i 'og tu dge tshul rnams la dgag dbye bya'o / /
de'i 'og tu dge slong rnams la'o / /
dge slong bzhi man chad kyis ni byin gyis brlab par bya'o / /
deng dge 'dun gyis dgag dbye bco lnga pa yin la /
bdag dge slong ming 'di zhes bya ba'i dgag dbye yang bco lnga pa yin te /
bdag dge slong ming 'di zhes bya bas dgag dbye byin gyis brlab bo / /
gang gi tshe dge 'dun tshogs pa de'i tshe bdag la mthong ba dang thos pa dang dogs pa'i gnas gsum gyis dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun la dgag dbye bya'o / /
lan gsum du bzlas /
dgag dbye'i gzhi'o // //
bam po brgyad pa /
sra brkyang gi gzhi'i sdom la /
sra brkyang gding bar byed pa dang / /
'ding dang go byed 'byin pa'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
'di ltar gnas 'di na dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyis gos kyi rnyed pa'i chos gos bgyis pa 'di dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang du bzhed na /
gal te dge 'dun gyis dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
'di lta ste /
gnas bsdu ba dang /
dge slong rnams bde ba la reg par gnas par bgyi ba dang /
sbyin pa po rnams kyi sbyin par bya ba'i chos yongs su spyad pa'i slad du chos gos sra brkyang du bgyis te /
gnas gang du sra brkyang bting bar chos gos rnying pa rnams dang yang mi 'bral na gsar pa rnams dang lta ci smos /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
'di ltar gnas 'dir dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyis gos kyi rnyed pa'i chos gos bgyis pa 'di dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang du bzhes pas /
de'i slad du 'di lta ste gnas bsdu ba dang /
dge slong rnams bde ba la reg par gnas par bgyi ba dang /
sbyin pa po rnams kyi sbyin par bya ba'i chos yongs su spyad pa'i slad du dge 'dun gyis chos gos 'di sra brkyang du bgyis te /
gnas gang du sra brkyang bting bar chos gos rnying pa rnams dang yang mi 'bral na gsar pa rnams dang lta ci smos te /
chos gos 'di sra brkyang du bgyi bar tshe dang ldan pa gang dag bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis chos gos 'di sra brkyang du bgyis lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
ming 'di zhes bya ba khyod dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar spro'am /
spro'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar spro na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyi dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar bsko ste /
dge slong sra brkyang 'ding ba ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar 'gyur ro / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar spro na /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar bsko ste /
dge slong sra brkyang 'ding ba ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar 'gyur na /
dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar bsko bar tshe dang ldan pa gang dag bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi bar dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar bskos lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
chos gos 'di ni dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang du blo mthun par bgyis pa lags /
dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di ni dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar bskos lags na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
'di lta ste gnas bsdu ba dang /
dge slong rnams bde ba la reg par gnas par bgyi ba dang /
sbyin pa po rnams kyi sbyin par bya ba'i chos yongs su spyad pa'i slad du dge 'dun gyi chos gos 'di sra brkyang 'ding ba dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba la gtod cing sra brkyang 'ding ba dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba chos gos 'dis dbyar gnas pa'i dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang 'ding bar 'gyur te /
gnas gang du sra brkyang bting bar chos gos rnying pa rnams dang yang mi 'bral na gsar pa rnams dang lta ci smos /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
chos gos 'di ni dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang du blo mthun par bgyis pa lags /
bdag dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba ni sra brkyang 'ding bar bskos lags te /
'di lta ste gnas bsdu ba dang /
dge slong rnams bde ba la reg par gnas par bgyi ba dang /
sbyin pa po rnams kyi sbyin par bya ba'i chos yongs su dpyad pa'i slad du bdag sra brkyang 'ding ba dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi bas chos gos 'di dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang gding bar bgyi'o / /
gnas gang du sra brkyang bting bar chos gos rnying pa rnams dang yang mi 'bral na gsar pa rnams dang lta ci smos /
lan gsum du bzlas /
gnas brtan nam btsun pa'am tshe dang ldan pa dgongs su gsol /
chos gos 'di ni dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang du blo mthun par bgyis pa lags /
bdag dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba ni sra brkyang 'ding bar bskos pa lags te /
de'i slad du 'di lta ste /
gnas bsdu ba dang /
dge slong rnams bde ba la reg par gnas par bgyi ba dang /
sbyin pa po rnams kyi sbyin par bya ba'i chos yongs su spyad pa'i slad du bdag sra brkyang 'ding ba dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi bas chos gos 'di dge 'dun gyi sra brkyang bting lags te /
gnas gang du sra brkyang bting bar chos gos rnying pa rnams dang yang mi 'bral na gsar pa rnams dang lta ci smos /
lan gsum bzlas /
legs par bting ngo / /
shin tu bting ngo / /
'di la rnyed pa dang phan yon gang yod pa de bdag gi yin no / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
'di ltar gnas 'dir dge slong gi dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang bting ba las de'i rjes su 'jug pa'i dus rdzogs te /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang 'byin pa mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
'di ltar gnas 'dir dge slong gi dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang bting ba las de'i rjes su 'jug pa'i dus rdzogs te /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang 'byin na /
sra brkyang 'byin par tshe dang ldan pa gang dag bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang phyung lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
'di ltar gnas 'dir dge slong gi dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang bting ba las chom rkun gyis bcom pa'i dge slong rnams lhags na gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
chom rkum gyis bcom pa'i dge slong rnams la brten te dge 'dun sra brkyang 'byin pa mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
'di ltar gnas 'dir dge slong gi dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang bting ba las chom rkun gyis bcom pa'i dge slong rnams lhags te /
de'i slad du chom rkun gyis bcom pa'i dge slong rnams la brten nas dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang 'byin pa mdzad na /
chom rkun gyis bcom pa'i dge slong rnams la brten te sra brkyang 'byin par tshe dang ldan pa gang dag bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas chom rkun gyis bcom pa'i dge slong rnams la brtan nas dge 'dun gyis sra brkyang phyung lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
sra brkyang gi gzhi'o // //
gos kyi gzhi dang nye ba'i gos kyi gzhi'i sdom la /
shi dang nor 'dra snod 'gyid dang / /
bcu gsum dang ni rung bya ba / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
'di ltar gnas 'dir dge slong nye dga' gum na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong nye dga' gum pa'i rdzas bgo bar bgyi ba gum pa'i yo byad chos gos dang chos gos ma lags pa gda' ba dang mi gda' ba byin gyis brlab bo / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
'di ltar gnas 'dir dge slong gre skyes gum par gyur na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong kun dga' bo nor dang 'dra bas dge slong gre skyes gum pa'i rdzas bgo bar bgyi ba gum pa'i yo byad chos gos dang chos gos ma lags pa gda' ba dang mi gda' ba byin gyis brlab bo / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
gos kyi gzhi'o // //
ming 'di zhes bya ba khyod dge 'dun gyi snod spyad 'gyed par spro'am /
spro'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dge 'dun gyi snod spyad 'gyed par spro na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dge 'dun gyi snod spyad 'gyed par bsko ste /
dge slong snod spyad 'gyed pa ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dge 'dun gyi snod spyad 'gyed par 'gyur ro / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dge 'dun gyi snod spyad 'gyed par spro ste /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba'i dge 'dun gyi snod spyad 'gyed par bsko ste /
dge slong snod spyad 'gyed pa ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dge 'dun gyi snod spyad 'gyed par 'gyur na tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dge 'dun gyi snod spyad 'gyed par bsko bar bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsung shig /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di dge 'dun snod spyad 'gyed par bskos lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
tshe dang ldan pa dgongs su gsol /
bdag ming 'di zhes bgyi ba'i chos gos bgyis lags pa rung ba spyad par 'os pa'i chos gos snam sbyar du byin gyis brlab bo / /
lan gsum du bzlas /
thabs yin no / /
legs so / /
de bzhin du bla gos dang /
mthang gos dang /
sham thabs dang /
sham thabs kyi gzan dang rdul gzan dang /
rngul gzan gyi gzan dang /
gdong phyis dang /
rnag gzan dang /
g.yan pa dgab pa dang /
skra bzed dang /
gding ba dang /
dbyar gyi gos ras chen la yang brjod par bya'o / /
tshe dang ldan pa dgongs su gsol /
gos 'di bdag dang grogs tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa la mkho ba'i yo byad kyi gos su byin gyis brlab bo / /
lan gsum du bzlas /
thabs yin no / /
legs so / /
tshe dang ldan pa dgongs su gsol /
bdag ming 'di zhes bgyi ba'i chos gos lhag pa rung bar ma bgyis pa rung bar bgyi bar 'os pa 'di mkhan po la rung bar bgyi'o / /
mkhan po la yid brtan te bcang bar bgyi'o / /
rkyen ji lta ba bzhin du bgyi'o / /
lan gsum du bzlas /
thabs yin no / /
legs so / /
gos kyi gzhi dang /
nye ba'i gos kyi gzhi'o // //
sman gyi gzhi dang las kyi gzhi'i sdom la /
sman dang rung ba'i khang pa dang / /
'dun pa'i gso sbyong bya ba'o / /
tshe dang ldan pa dgongs su gsol / /
bdag dge slong ming 'di zhes bgyi ba'i sman thun tshod du rung ba 'di dag bdag dang tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa rnams kyir bgyi bar thun tshod du rung bar byin gyis brlab bo / /
lan gsum bzlas /
thabs yin no / /
legs so / /
zhag bdun pa dang /
'tsho ba'i bar du bcang ba dag la yang de bzhin no / /
dge slong lag gi blas rdo bteg pa na de'i dang por gzhi 'di ni dge 'dun gyi rung ba'i khang par 'gyur ba'o snyam du sems bskyed par bya zhing tshig tu yang brjod par bya'o / /
dge slong rab tu mang po dag gis sems bsdu bas tshe dang ldan pa dag gzhi 'di ni dge 'dun gyi rung ba'i khang par 'gyur bar sems sdus shig ces sems bsdu bar bya'o / /
dge slong ji snyed der phyin pa thams cad kyis gzhi 'di ni dge 'dun gyi rung ba'i khang par 'gyur ba'o / /
zhes tshig mthun par cig car brjod par bya'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
gnas thams cad grub pa'am bgyis pa'am lags pa nang mtshams dang phyi rol nye 'khor 'dom gang dang bcas pa 'di dge 'dun gyi rung ba'i khang par bzhed na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyi gnas thams cad grub pa'am bgyis pa'am lags pa nang mtshams dang phyi rol nye 'khor 'dom gang bcas pa 'di dge 'dun gyi rung ba'i khang par bgyi'o / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
gnas thams cad grub pa'am bgyis pa'am lags pa nang mtshams dang phyi rol nye 'khor 'dom gang bcas pa 'di dge 'dun gyi rung ba'i khang par bzhed de /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyi gnas thams cad grub pa'am bgyis pa'am lags pa nang mtshams dang phyi rol nye 'khor 'dom gang dang bcas pa 'di dge 'dun gyi rung ba'i khang par bgyid na tshe dang ldan pa gang dag gnas thams cad grub pa'am bgyis pa 'am lags pa nang mtshams dang phyi rol nye 'khor 'dom gang dang bcas pa 'di dge 'dun gyi rung ba'i khang par bgyi bar bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyi gnas thams cad grub pa'am bgyis pa'am lags pa nang mtshams dang phyi rol nye 'khor 'dom gang dang bcas pa 'di dge 'dun gyi rung ba'i khang par bgyis lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
sman gyi gzhi'o // //
'phags pa dgongs su gsol / /
rgyal po'i kun dga' ra ba'i dge slong ma'i dge 'dun mthun pa rgyal byed kyi tshal gyi dge slong gi dge 'dun mthun pa'i zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal lo / /
gnod pa nyung ngam /
nyam nga ba chung ngam /
bskyod pa yang ngam /
'tsho'am /
stobs dang ldan nam /
bde ba'am /
kha na ma tho ba ma mchis sam /
bde ba la reg par gnas sam zhes bsnyun gsol lo / /
zla ba phyed phyed cing gdams ngag dang rjes su bstan pa gsol lo / /
'dun pa dang gso sbyong bgyi bar gsol ba 'debs so / /
gsol ba yang mkhyen par gsol lo / /
las kyi gzhi'o // //
phyir bcos pa'i gzhi'i sdom la /
gleng dang nan tur bzod pa dang / /
mthol dang spo ba rnams dang ni / /
mgu dang dbyung bar bya ba'o / /
tshe dang ldan pa ming 'di zhes bya ba khyod re lde ri la song ste /
dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so la dge sbyong gi chos ma yin pa rnam pa mang pos gleng bar spro'am /
spro'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong gleng ba po ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di re lde ri la song ste /
dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so la dge sbyong gi chos ma lags pa mang pos gleng bar spro na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong gleng ba po ming 'di zhes bgyi ba dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so la gleng bar bsko'o / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong gleng ba po ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di re lde ri la mchis nas dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so la dge sbyong gi chos ma lags pa rnam mang pos gleng bar spro ste /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong gleng ba po ming 'di zhes bgyi ba dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so la gleng bar bsko na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong gleng ba po ming 'di zhes bgyi ba dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so la gleng bar bsko ba bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong gleng ba po ming 'di zhes bgyi ba dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so la gleng bar bskos lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsungs bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dmar ser can 'di dag ni 'thab krol bgyid pa /
mtshang 'bru bar bgyid pa /
rtsod par bgyid pa /
'gyed par bgyid pa /
rtsod pa'i gzhi bgyid pa lags te /
de dag dge slong rnams la rgyun du rtsod pa'i gzhi bskyed pas des na lung mnod pa dang /
klag pa dang /
kha ton bgyid pa dang /
rnal 'byor dang /
yid la bgyi ba dang /
nang du sems zhi gnas su bgyi ba shor na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong dmar ser can 'thab krol bgyid pa ma btang ba rnams la bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dmar ser can 'di ni 'thab krol bgyid pa /
mtshang 'bru bar bgyid pa /
rtsod par bgyid pa /
'gyed par bgyid pa /
rtsod pa'i gzhi bgyid pa lags te /
de dag dge slong rnams la rgyun tu rtsod pa'i gzhi skyed pas /
des na dge 'dun lung mnod pa dang /
klag pa dang /
kha ton bgyi ba dang /
rnal 'byor dang /
yid la bgyi ba dang /
nang du sems zhi gnas su bgyi ba shor na /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong dmar ser can 'thab krol bgyid pa ma btang ba rnams la bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong dmar ser can 'thab krol ma btang ba rnams la bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsungs shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong dmar ser can 'thab krol bgyid pa ma btang ba rnams la bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
bdag dge slong dmar ser can 'thab krol bgyid pa /
mtshang 'bru bar bgyid pa /
rtsod par bgyid pa /
'gyed par bgyid pa /
rtsod pa'i gzhi bgyid pa lags pas /
dge 'dun gyis bdag la bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
bdag dge slong dmar ser can bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la /
mtshams kyi nang du mchis te bzod pa gsol zhing 'thab krol bgyid pa de yang spong na /
thugs brtse ba can dge 'dun btsun pa rnams kyis thugs brtse ba'i slad du /
bdag dge slong dmar ser can bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad du gsol /
lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dmar ser can 'di 'thab krol bgyid pa /
mtshang 'bru bar bgyid pa /
rtsod par bgyid pa /
'gyed par bgyid pa /
rtsod pa'i gzhi bgyid pa lags pas 'thab krol bgyid pa ma btang ba 'di la dge 'dun gyis bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
'di bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing /
dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la mtshams kyi nang du mchis te /
bzod pa gsol zhing 'thab krol bgyid pa de yang spong ngo zhes mchi na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong dmar ser can bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dmar ser can ming 'di zhes bgyi ba 'di 'thab krol bgyid pa /
mtshang 'bru bar bgyid pa /
rtsod par bgyid pa /
'gyed par bgyid pa /
rtsod pa'i gzhi bgyid pa lags pas 'thab krol bgyid pa ma btang ba 'di la dge 'dun gyis bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
'di bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la mtshams kyi nang du mchis te bzod pa gsol zhing 'thab krol bgyid pa de yang spong ste /
de'i slad du dge slong dmar ser can ming 'di zhes bgyi ba dge 'dun gyis bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong dmar ser can bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa ming 'di zhes bgyi ba la bzod pa mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong dmar ser can bsdigs pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa ming 'di zhes bgyi ba la bzod pa mdzad lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dge ldan ltung ba rgyun tu bgyid pa 'di dge 'dun lhag ma'i ltung ba rgyun du bgyid de /
'di la dge 'dun gyis spo ba dang /
gzhi nas spo ba dang /
mgu bar bgyi ba dang /
gzhi nas mgu bar bgyi ba stsol ba dang 'byin pa mdzad pas /

dge 'dun gyis dge slong dge ldan ltung ba rgyun du bgyid pa la smad pa'i phrin las mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dge ldan ltung ba rgyun tu bgyid pa 'di dge 'dun lhag ma'i ltung ba rgyun du bgyid de /
'di la dge 'dun gyis spo ba dang gzhi nas spo ba dang /
mgu bar bgyi ba dang gzhi nas mgu bar bgyi ba stsol ba dang 'byin pa mdzad pas lung mnod pa dang /

bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /

'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
bdag dge slong dge ldan ltung ba rgyun du 'byin pa la dge 'dun lhag ma'i ltung ba rgyun du 'byin pas bdag la dge 'dun gyis smad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
bdag dge slong dge ldan ltung ba rgyun tu bgyid pa la smad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la mtshams kyi nang du mchis te /
bzod pa gsol zhing ltung ba rgyun du bgyid pa de yang spong na /
thugs brtse ba can dge 'dun btsun pa rnams kyis thugs brtse ba'i slad du bdag dge slong dge ldan smad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad du gsol /
lan gsum du bzlas dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dge 'dun 'di ltung ba rgyun tu bgyid de /
'di dge 'dun lhag ma'i ltung ba rgyun du bgyis pas 'di la dge 'dun gyis spo ba dang /
gzhi nas spo ba dang /
mgu bar bgyi ba dang /
gzhi nas mgu bar bgyi ba stsol ba dang 'byin pa mdzad pas lung mnod pa dang /
klag pa dang /

yid la bgyi ba dang /
nang du sems zhi gnas su bgyi ba shor te /

'di la smad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /

bzod pa gsol zhing ltung ba rgyun du bgyid pa de'ang spong ngo zhes mchi na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong dge ldan smad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /

dge slong dge ldan ltung ba rgyun du bgyid pa 'di dge 'dun lhag ma'i ltung ba rgyun du bgyid de /

dge slong dge ldan 'di smad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la mtshams kyi nang du mchis te /
bzod pa gsol zhing ltung ba rgyun du bgyid pa de yang spong ngo zhes mchi na /
de'i slad du dge slong dge ldan smad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la dge 'dun gyis bzod pa mdzad na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong dge ldan smad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong dge ldan smad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so 'di gnyis khyim sun 'byin pa sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod pa lags te /
'di gnyis khyim sun 'byin par yang snang zhing thos la 'tshal /
'di gnyis sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod par yang snang zhing thos la 'tshal na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so khyim sun 'byin pa ma btang ba la bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so 'di gnyis khyim sun 'byin pa sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod pa lags te /
'di gnyis khyim sun 'byin par yang snang zhing thos la 'tshal /
sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod par yang snang zhing thos la 'tshal te /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so khyim sun 'byin pa ma btang ba la bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so la bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so khyim sun 'byin pa ma btang ba la bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
bdag cag dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so khyim sun 'byin pa sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod pa lags pas bdag cag la dge 'dun gyis bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
bdag cag dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing /
dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la /
mtshams kyi nang du mchis te bzod pa gsol zhing khyim sun 'byin pa sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod pa de yang spong na /
thugs brtse ba can dge 'dun btsun pa rnams kyis thugs brtse ba'i slad du bdag cag dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad du gsol /
lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so 'di gnyis khyim sun 'byin pa sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod pa lags te /
'di gnyis khyim sun 'byin par snang zhing thos la 'tshal /
'di gnyis sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod par yang snang zhing thos la 'tshal te /
khyim sun 'byin pa sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod pa ma btang ba 'di gnyis la dge 'dun gyis bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
'di gnyis bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la /
mtshams kyi nang du mchis te bzod pa gsol zhing khyim sun 'byin pa sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod pa de yang spong ngo zhes mchi na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la dge 'dun gyis bzod pa mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so 'di gnyis khyim sun 'byin pa sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod pas /
'di gnyis la dge 'dun gyis bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la mtshams kyi nang du mchis te bzod pa gsol zhing khyim sun 'byin pa sdig pa'i chos kun tu spyod pa de yang spong ngo zhes mchis pa la bzod pa mdzad na tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shing / /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'gro mgyogs dang nab so bskrad pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dam pa 'di khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid na gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong dam pa khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pa la slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dam pa 'di khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid de /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong dam pa khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pa la slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong dam pa khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pa la slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong dam pa khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pa la slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
bdag dge slong dam pa khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pas bdag la dge 'dun gyis slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
bdag dge slong dam pa slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la mtshams kyi nang du mchis te bzod pa gsol zhing khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pa de yang spong na /
thugs brtse ba can dge 'dun btsun pa rnams kyis thugs brtse ba'i slad du bdag dge slong dam pa la slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad du gsol /
lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dam pa 'di khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pa de la dge 'dun gyis slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
'di ltar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la mtshams kyi nang du mchis te /
bzod pa gsol zhing khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pa de yang spong ngo zhes mchi na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge slong dam pa slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la dge 'dun gyis bzod pa mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong dam pa 'di khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pas de la dge 'dun gyis slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong dam pa skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la /
mtshams kyi nang du mchis te bzod pa gsol zhing khyim pa la brnyas thabs bgyid pa /
de'ang spong ngo zhes mchi ba la bzod pa mdzad na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong dam pa slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong dam pa slar 'gyed pa'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'dun pa 'di la ltung ba byung ste /
de la dge slong rnams kyis glengs shing dran par bgyis kyang ltung ba ma mthong ngo zhes mchi na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'dun pa ltung ba ma mthong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzod do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'dun pa 'di la ltung ba byung ste /
de la dge slong rnams kyis glengs shing dran par bgyis kyang ltung ba ma mthong ngo zhes mchis te /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'dun pa ltung ba ma mthong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong 'dun pa la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'dun pa ltung ba ma mthong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
bdag dge slong 'dun pa la ltung ba byung bas dge 'dun gyis bdag 'dun pa ltung ba ma mthong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
bdag dge slong 'dun pa ltung ba ma mthong bas gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la mtshams kyi nang du mchis te /
bzod pa gsol zhing ltung ba de yang mthong na /

lan gsum du bzlas /

tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong 'dun pa ltung ba ma mthong bas gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /

'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'dun pa 'di la ltung ba byung yang de chos bzhin du slar mi 'chos na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'dun pa ltung ba slar mi 'chos pa de la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'dun pa 'di ltung ba byung yang de chos bzhin du slar mi 'chos pas /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'dun pa ltung ba chos bzhin du slar mi 'chos pa 'di la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad na /

gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /

'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
bdag dge slong 'dun pa ltung ba byung la ltung ba de chos bzhin du slar mi 'chos pas /
bdag ltung ba slar mi 'chos pa la dge 'dun gyis gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags te /
bdag dge slong 'dun pa slar mi 'chos pa gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags pas skra 'greng bar gyur /

lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /

dge slong 'dun pa slar mi 'chos pas gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags pas 'di skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la /
mtshams kyi nang du mchis te /
bzod pa gsol zhing ltung ba de yang chos bzhin du slar 'chos so zhes mchi na /

'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'dun pa 'di la ltung ba byung ste /

dge slong 'dun pa slar mi 'chos pas gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags pa 'di skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston /
mtshams kyi nang du mchis te bzod pa gsol zhing slar 'chos so zhes mchis pas /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'dun pa slar mi 'chos pas gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong 'dun pa slar mi 'chos pas gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad par bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'dun pa slar mi 'chos pas gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'chi ltas 'di la sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di byung ste /
ji ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis bar du gcod pa'i chos su gsungs pa gang dag yin pa de dag brten kyang bar du gcod par mi 'gyur te /
de ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis chos bstan pa bdag gis shes so zhes mchi nas 'di la dge slong rab tu mang pos bzhams te bsgo na /
'di la dge slong rab tu mang pos bzhams te bsgo yang sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa de nyid la nan gyis mchog tu bzung zhing mngon par zhen nas 'di nyid bden gyi gzhan ni brdzun pa'o zhes rjes su tha snyad 'dogs te /
'di la dge 'dun gyis gsol ba dang bzhi'i las kyis bsgo na /
'di la gsol ba dang bzhi'i las kyis bsgo yang sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa de nyid la nan gyis mchog tu bzung zhing mngon par zhen nas 'di nyid bden gyi gzhan ni brdzun pa'o zhes rjes su tha snyad 'dogs na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa mi gtong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las bgyis te /
ji srid du dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di thams cad kyi thams cad dang /
rnam pa thams cad kyi thams cad du mi gtong ba de srid du gtam 'dre bar mi bgyi /
phebs par smra bar mi bgyi zhing dper na gdol bu bzhin du smad par bgyi zhing mchog tu smad par bgyi'o / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'chi ltas 'di la sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di byung ste /
'di ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis bar du gcod pa'i chos su gsungs pa gang dag yin pa de dag brten kyang bar du gcod par mi 'gyur te /
de ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis chos bstan pa bdag gis shes so zhes mchi nas 'di la dge slong rab tu mang pos bzhams te bsgo na /
'di la dge slong rab tu mang pos bzhams te bsgo yang sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa de nyid la nan gyis mchog tu bzung zhing mngon par zhen nas 'di nyid bden gyi gzhan ni brdzun pa'o zhes rjes su tha snyad 'dogs te /
'di la dge 'dun gyis gsol ba dang bzhi'i las kyis bsgo na /
'di la gsol ba dang bzhi'i las kyis bsgo yang sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa de nyid la nan gyis mchog tu bzung zhing mngon par zhen nas /
'di nyid bden gyis gzhan ni brdzun pa'o zhes rjes su tha snyad 'dogs pa de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa mi gtong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i las bgyi ste /
ji srid du dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di thams cad kyi thams cad dang /
rnam pa thams cad kyi thams cad mi gtong ba de srid du gtam 'dre bar mi bgyi phebs par smra bar mi bgyi zhing dper na gdol bu bzhin du smad par bgyi zhing mchog tu smad par bgyid na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa mi gtong ba la ni gnas nas dbyung ba'i las bgyi zhing ji srid du dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di thams cad kyi thams cad dang rnam pa thams cad kyi thams cad du mi gtong ba de srid du gtam 'dre bar mi bgyi /
phebs par smra bar mi bgyi zhing dper na gdol bu bzhin du smad par bgyi zhing mchog tu smad par bgyi bar bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa mi gtong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad cing ji srid du dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di thams cad kyi thams cad dang rnam pa thams cad kyi thams cad du mi gtong ba de srid du gtam 'dre bar mi bgyi /
phebs par smra bar mi bgyi zhing /
dper na gdol bu bzhin du smad par bgyis shing mchog tu smad par bgyis lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
bdag dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di byung ste /
ji ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis bar du gcod pa'i chos su gsungs pa gang dag yin pa de dag brten kyang bar du gcod par mi 'gyur te /
de ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis chos bstan pa bdag gis shes so zhes mchis pas dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa mi gtong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad cing smad lags te /
bdag dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa mi gtong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad cing smad lags pas skra 'greng par gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs bar nye bar ston la /
mtshams kyi nang du mchis te bzod pa gsol zhing sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa de yang gtong na /
thugs brtse ba can dge 'dun btsun pa rnams kyis thugs brtse ba'i slad du bdag dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa btang lags pa la bzod pa mdzad du gsol /
lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'chi ltas 'di la sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di byung ste /
ji ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis bar du gcod pa'i chos su gsungs pa gang dag yin pa de dag brten kyang bar du gcod par mi 'gyur te /
de ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis chos bstan pa bdag gis shes so zhes mchi nas /
dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa mi gtong ba 'di la dge 'dun gyis gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad cing smad lags te /
dge slong 'chi ltas gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad cing smad pa 'di skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la mtshams kyi nang du 'chis te bzod pa gsol zhing sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa de yang gtong ngo zhes mchi na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa mi gtong ba la gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad cing smad lags pa la bzod pa mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong 'chi ltas 'di la sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa 'di lta bu 'di byung ste /
ji ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis bar du gcod pa'i chos su gsungs pa gang dag yin pa de dag brten kyang bar du gcod par mi 'gyur te /
de ltar bcom ldan 'das kyis chos bstan pa bdag gis shes so zhes mchi nas de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong 'chi ltas sdig pa can gyi lta ba'i rnam pa mi gtong ba 'di gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad cing smad lags te /
dge slong 'chi ltas gnas nas dbyung ba'i phrin las mdzad cing smad lags pas 'di skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid /
'byung bar bskyod /

tshe dang ldan pa gyad bu nor la yang dag pa ma lags pas skur te /
dge 'dun gyis de la lhung bzed khas dbub pa mdzad lags pa las /
li ts+tsha bI chen pos lhung bzed khas phub pa de'i dge 'dun las lhung bzed slar bzlog pa gsol na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis li ts+tsha bI chen po las lhung bzed slar bzlog pa mdzad do / /
'di ni gsol ba'o / /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
bdag dge slong dga' byed kyis bslab pa ma phul bar mi tshangs par spyod pa 'khrig pa'i chos bsten kyang bcab pa'i sems gcig tsam gyis kyang bcabs par ma bgyis te /
bdag dge slong dga' byed dge 'dun la ji srid 'tsho'i bar du bslab pa gsol na /

dge slong dga' byed 'di dge 'dun las ji srid 'tsho'i bar du bslab pa gsol na /

rtsod pa dang /
'gyed pa byung pa'i gzhi ni 'di lta ste /
ltung ba byung ngam ma byung ba dang /
gnas nas phyung ngam ma phyung ba lags na /
bdag cag la ltung ba byung gi ltung ba ma byung ba ma lags /
gnas nas phyung ba lags kyi gnas nas ma phyung ba ma lags te /
gang gnas nas phyung ba ni chos dang mthun pa'i phrin las ma 'khrugs par gzhag par mi 'os pa bgyis so snyam bgyis nas /
bdag grong khyer yangs pa can gyi dge slong dang sdums bgyi zhing mthun par bgyi'o snyam ste /
bdag kau shAm+bI pa'i dge slong skra 'greng bar gyur /
skra 'phyar bar gyur cing dge 'dun la spu snyol bar bgyid na /

'byung bar bskyod /
mtshungs par nye bar ston la /

dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /

smra bar ma bsams kyang smras te /
bdag gis dran pa rnyed na bdag la dge slong rnams kyis gzhi des gleng bas bdag dge slong bye ma skyes dge 'dun la ma smyos pas 'dul ba gsol na /
thugs brtse ba can dge 'dun btsun pa rnams kyis thugs brtse ba'i slad du bdag dge slong bye ma skyes la ma smyos pas 'dul ba stsal du gsol /
lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong bye ma skyes smyos pa sems 'khrugs pa sdug bsngal gyi tshor bas gzir ba 'dis dge sbyong gi tshul ma lags pa /
rjes su mthun pa ma lags pa /
rung ba ma lags pa /
tshul dang mthun pa ma lags pa mang du spyad cing smras te stsal nas mig 'gyur /
kha chu zags /
bzhin bsgyur /
sa la 'gres ldogs /
gnyid kyis ma log kyang gnyid kyis log pa ltar bcos /
ma smyos kyang smyos pa ltar bcos /
smra bar ma bsams kyang smras te /
'dis dran pa rnyed na 'di la dge slong rnams kyis gzhi des gleng bas dge slong bye ma skyes 'di dge 'dun las ma smyos par 'dul ba gsol na /
gal te dge 'dun gyi dus la bab cing bzod na dge 'dun gyis gnang bar mdzod cig dang /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong bye ma skyes la ma smyos pas 'dul ba stsol to / /
'di ni gsol ba'o /
dge 'dun btsun pa rnams gsan du gsol /
dge slong bye ma skyes smyos pa sems 'khrugs pa /
sdug bsngal gyi tshor bas gzir ba 'dis dge sbyong gi tshul ma lags pa /
rjes su mthun pa ma lags pa /
rung ba ma lags pa /
tshul dang mthun pa ma lags pa /
mang du spyad cing smras te stsal nas mig 'gyur /
kha chu zags /
bzhin bsgyur /
sa la 'gres ldogs /
gnyid kyis ma log kyang gnyis kyis log pa ltar bcos /
ma smyos kyang smyos pa ltar bcos /
smra bar ma bsams kyang smras te /
'dis dran pa rnyed na 'di la dge slong rnams kyis gzhi des gleng bas dge slong bye ma skyes 'di dge 'dun las ma smyos pas 'dul ba gsol te /
de'i slad du dge 'dun gyis dge slong bye ma skyes la ma smyos pas 'dul ba gsol na /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag dge slong bye ma skyes la ma smyos pas /
'dul ba stsal bar bzod pa de dag ni cang ma gsung shig /
gang dag mi bzod pa de dag ni gsungs shig /
'di ni las brjod pa dang po ste /
de bzhin du lan gnyis lan gsum du bzlas /
dge 'dun gyis bzod cing gnang nas /
dge 'dun gyis dge slong bye ma skyes la ma smyos pas 'dul ba stsal lags te /
'di ltar cang mi gsung bas de de bzhin du 'dzin to / /
tshe dang ldan pa gang dag bdag cag legs par gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba la rab tu byung nas 'thab par gyur /
mtshang 'bru bar gyur /
rtsod par gyur /
'gyed par gyur cing gnas te /
phyogs dang gzhan gyi phyogs su rnam par gnas pa ni bdag cag gis ma rnyed de /
rnyed pa ma yin no / /
nyes pa rnyed kyi legs par rnyed pa ni ma yin no / /
kha na ma tho ba sbom po dang /
khyim na gnas pa la ston pa ma gtogs par gzhi 'di las khyod la ltung ba byung ba gang yin pa dang /
bdag la ltung ba byung ba gang yin pa de dag tshe dang ldan pa gang dag gi mdun du mthol ba dang /
'chags pa dang /
mi 'chab par bdag spro'o / /
tshe dang ldan pa dag bdag cag legs par gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba la rab tu byung nas 'thab par gyur /
mtshang 'bru bar gyur /
rtsod par gyur /
'gyed par gyur cing gnas te /
phyogs dang gzhan gyi phyogs su rnam par gnas pa ni bdag cag gis ma rnyed de /
rnyed pa ma yin no / /
nyes pa rnyed kyis legs pa ma rnyed de /
kha na ma tho ba sbom po dang /
khyim na gnas pa la ston pa ma gtogs par gzhi 'di las khyed cag la ltung ba byung ba gang yin pa dang /
bdag la ltung ba byung ba gang yin pa de dag tshe dang ldan pa dag gi mdun du bdag mthol lo / /
bshags so / /
mi 'chab bo / /
mthol zhing bshags na bdag bde ba la reg par gnas par 'gyur ro / /
ma mthol ma bshags na ni mi 'gyur ro / /
lan gsum du bzlas /
ltung ba mthong ngam /
mthong ngo / /
phyin cad sdom mam /
sdom mo / /
lan gsum du bzlas /
rtsod pa'i gzhi'o // //
gnas mal gyi gzhi dang nye ba'i gzhi'i sdom la /
gnas khang zas la bsko ba gnyis / /
thug pa bag chos 'brim pa gnyis / /
phran tshegs 'brim par byed pa gnyis / /
snod spyad 'brub pa dang gos kyi gnyis / /
dbyar gyi ras chen sped dang 'gyed / /
mngag gzhug pa dang mdzes chos te / /
gang zag bcu dang gnyis po dag /
ston pas yang dag bshad pa yin / /
lag gi bla dang lag dpon dang / /

las kyi grangs brgya rtsa gcig tu nges par gang las shes she na /
gtam gyi gzhi las las kyi grangs brjod pa la /
btsun pa las dag tu mchis /
nye ba 'khor brgya rtsa gcig go /
btsun pa las du dag gis las thams cad bsdus /
nye ba 'khor gsum gyis te /
gsum gang zhe na /
gsol ba'i las dang /
gsol ba dang gnyis kyi las dang /
gsol ba dang bzhi'i las kyis so / /
btsun pa las brgya rtsa gcig po gang dag lags pa de dag ni gsol ba'i las dag ni du /
gsol ba dang gnyis kyi las dag ni du /
gsol ba dang bzhi'i las dag ni du mchis bka' stsal pa nye ba 'khor /
gsol ba'i las ni nyi shu rtsa bzhi'o / /
gsol ba dang gnyis kyi las ni bzhi bcu rtsa bdun no / /
gsol ba dang bzhi'i las ni sum cu'o zhes gsungs so / /
de las gsol ba'i las nyi shu rtsa bzhi gang zhe na /
gal te gsang ste ston pa'i slob dpon gyis bar chad kyi chos rnams gsang ste dri ba'i phyir gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
las byed pa'i slob dpon gyis bar chad kyi chos rnams dge 'dun gyi nang du dri ba'i phyir gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
so sor thar pa'i mdo 'don pa'i phyir gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
gso sbyong de la dge 'dun thams cad ltung ba dang bcas par gyur na gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
gso sbyong gi tshe ltung ba de la dge 'dun thams cad yid gnyis dang bcas par gyur na gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
gso sbyong gi tshe dge 'dun ltung ba'i phyir rtsod par gyur na gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
gso sbyong gi tshe ltung ba de ni gang yin pa de las ji ltar ni ldang bar 'gyur zhes bya ba la sogs pas nyes pa nyid ma yin par gyur na de'i tshe gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
dgag dbye bya ba'i phyir gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
dgag dbye de la dge 'dun thams cad ltung ba dang bcas par gyur na gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
dgag dbye'i tshe ltung ba de la dge 'dun thams cad yid gnyis dang bcas par gyur na gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
dgag dbye'i tshe dge 'dun ltung ba'i phyir rtsod par gyur na gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
dgag dbye'i tshe ltung ba de ni gang yin de las ji ltar ni ldang bar 'gyur zhes bya ba la sogs pas nges pa nyid ma yin par gyur na de'i tshe gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
dbyar gnas par khas blang ba'i tshe gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
shi ba'i rdzas dang /

gyad bu nor lta bu chos gos gsum ngan pa la dge 'dun gyis ras yug chen sbyin pa la gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
dge slong dang dge slong ma gang dag ji ltar skye bo phal po che'i tshogs ma dad par rig par 'gyur ba de lta de ltar khyim rnams su spyod par byed pa khyim rnams su so sor go bar byed du gzhug pa la gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /
ngor 'phya ba'i grangs su gzhug pa la gsol ba 'ba' zhig gi las bya ba dang /

'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra pa'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po bram ze'i btsun pa slob dpon yon tan 'od bdag dang gzhan gyi grub pa'i mtha' rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son pa /

'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba kun las btus pa rdzogs so // //
dbang phyug dam pa'i mnga' bdag dpal lha btsan po'i bka' lung gis 'phags pa gzhi thams cad yod par smra ba'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa kha che'i bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang /
